What I didn‚Äôt like, because of the high humidity in Hangzhou, the room was a little smelly. I think they need a better air-conditioning to absorb all the humidity. We also booked a Non-Smoking room, and the guy at the check-in said there are all non-smoking rooms. When we went into the room it did not smell like smoke, but there was a ashtray on the office table and in the sofa there was a little burned whole from a cigarette - which seems a little strange for a non-smoking room. For the breakfast you had buffet style with very nice fresh juices and you could also choose from dishes a-la-carte. The location is ok, small shops and a bakery is next door and its a 30 min walk to the Westlake. Next time I personally would book a hotel directly on the lakeside with a nice view.

It is very comfortable. I took a nap on the sofa next to the bed and did not feel the light was dazzling at all.

It was a very good experience, probably because of the good weather in Hangzhou, which gave this hotel extra points. Until we got back to the hotel at 3 o'clock, the front desk didn't call us for 3 hours. In fact, the room has already been cleaned up. If we inform us early, we can check in early!
The table for taking meals for breakfast is too full. Many dishes are covered with large lids. When I took the food, there was a dish with a super large lid, and there was nowhere to put it. There was a statue standing next to it. The male waiter had clearly seen me at a loss, but ignored it.
In addition, there are free drinks next to the hotel elevator, which was a good thing, but no one told me during the whole process, and I saw it when I checked out!

2. Let's talk about hygiene, which is very bad
I have found the last guest in several places in the room, or the last guest, or the last guest left with long hair. After wiping the bath towel, I put it on the edge of the bathtub and found the hair. Silk, I feel disgusting. This shouldn't be the sanitary condition that a five-star hotel should have.

3. About room hardware
If it weren‚Äôt for modern technology products such as coffee machines and televisions in the room, I would really think that this hotel is a time passage leading to the 70s and 80s. Take a look at this toiletry bag, it looks broken and dirty, and there is also a "for use only" (do not take away) sign next to it. Please, isn't this funny? Such a tattered bag will not be picked up if you throw it on the street and pick it up, right?
Take a look at this lampshade. It has been sewn and repaired for three years. The mold on the lampshade, you must not have imagined that it was placed on your bedside.
There is also this curtain. Sunlight comes in after 6 o'clock in the morning. Can a five-star hotel not even be able to afford thicker fabrics? Can't open the pot at home?
In addition, there are many problems, such as whether the air conditioner is not cold, there is a slight musty smell in the room, and the carpet in the room looks dirty, so I won‚Äôt repeat them one by one.

4. Finally, let‚Äôs talk about breakfast
The breakfast is in the form of ordering + buffet, it is no problem to eat! The order is limited to one serving per person, because the order is limited to one, I think the quality should be good, but in fact the ingredients and taste are disappointing. I ordered egg sausage with salmon, "salmon" is used The domestic rainbow trout is shoddy, it has no salmon taste at all, nor does it have the unique white fat line of salmon. The pork sausage is not cooked, because the middle is red and bloody, and it is not chewy, so it looks like the restaurant foreman. The male waiter reacted. He insisted that his pork sausage is like this. This is what it should be. I didn‚Äôt say that I want to serve it again. It‚Äôs just that my friends and I have eaten it and feel unfamiliar.
